There is another  pool off to the side which is shallow and would be great for smaller children.  It is the perfect combination of indoor but with natural light and you can see the garden.  It is clean and well maintained.  Staff was extremely helpful but their English is limited so it is helpful to know some Chinese. My Chinese is limited but we managed just fine.

msg:I took my parents to stay in this hotel near Emerald Lake. The check-in lobby is in the main building No. 3, and we stayed in building No. 6. Although it was a bit inconvenient, the hotel has a car to drop off guests. The swimming pool and breakfast are both in the main building No. 3. Overall, the view of the Emerald Lake next door and the fairly thoughtful service made up for the shortcomings of the slightly outdated hardware facilities. The room was relatively quiet, and the breakfast was a bit lacking in quality, especially the dining table and the overall layout. There is still a lot of room for improvement. In fact, for an upscale hotel, breakfast is still very important. The pleasant surprise is that my alma mater, Anhui University, is across the street. I didn't notice this when I made the reservation. I hope to come back and stay in the future. The hotel has improved a lot.
